        - text: "At the end of the Thanksgiving Prayer, the Verses of the Cymbals are chanted:"
        - list [ref=f4e310]:
          - listitem [ref=f4e311]: From Sunday-Tuesday, the Adam days, the Verses of the Cymbals begin with "O come let us worship (Ⲁⲙⲱⲓⲛⲓ ⲙⲁⲣⲉⲛⲟⲩⲱϣⲧ)"
          - listitem [ref=f4e312]: From Wednesday-Saturday, the Watos days, the Verses of the Cymbals begin with "We worship the Father (Ⲧⲉⲛⲟⲩⲱϣⲧ ⲙ̀Ⲫ̀ⲓⲱⲧ)"
          - listitem [ref=f4e313]: The congregation continue the Verses of the Cymbals, mentioning verses for the saint of the church and any special occasion, and conclude the hymn.
      - generic [ref=f4e315]: On Adam days (Sunday through Tuesday), the people say the following.
